# Release v1.5.0 -- Maestro Harvest

> **Released**: 2026-05-10
> **Previous release**: [v1.4.0](RELEASE_v1.4.0.md)

---

## Full Changelog

### Added

- **T874b â€” Wire g-skl-graphify into g-go-code Step b0 (opt-in)** (2026-05-10): Step b0 of `g-go-code` is now split into b0.1 (gitnexus_impact, default-on) and b0.2 (graphify code-graph query, opt-in). Backend fallback order documented: gitNexus MCP â†’ graphify CLI â†’ tree-sitter+ripgrep. Failure modes (missing backend / graph staleness / query timeout / empty result) all degrade to legacy grep-based context-prep without halting the run. New `context_reduction_mode.graphify_b0_enabled` flag added to `.gald3r/config/AGENT_CONFIG.md` (safe default `false`). Cursor + Claude `g-go-code.md` parity surfaces updated together. Evidence + token-reduction delta documented in `docs/20260510_120000_Cursor_T874B_GRAPHIFY_B0_EVIDENCE.md`. Closes T874 AC3 deferred wiring.

- **T932 â€” Anthropic Financial Services Architecture: Vertical Bundle + Per-Agent MCP Scoping Pattern** (2026-05-09): Architectural analysis document at `docs/20260509_160000_Cursor_ANTHROPIC_FINANCIAL_AGENTS_ARCHITECTURE.md` studying the Anthropic `claude-for-financial-services` repo (Apache 2.0, 11.4k stars, restructured 2026-05-05). Documents three patterns: (1) **Vertical plugin bundles** â€” skill packs per business domain with `BUNDLE.md` manifests syncing into named agent folders via `sync_agent_skills.py`; (2) **Per-agent `.mcp.json` allowlist** â€” strict connector scoping preventing agents from accessing unregistered tools; (3) **`check.py` manifest linter** â€” validates agent structure, connector declarations, and broken paths at lint time. Includes gald3r vs Anthropic comparison table, adoption recommendations (adopt-now: `BUNDLE.md` manifests + `check_agents.ps1` linter; defer: per-agent MCP scoping migration, full subfolder agent structure), and `orchestrate.py` event loop analysis mapped to gald3r's `g-go` phases.

- **T907 â€” g-git-push SCA Compliance Gate Extension** (2026-05-09): Added optional `## Optional Compliance Gate` section to `.cursor/commands/g-git-push.md` and parity copy `.claude/commands/g-git-push.md`. Gate is opt-in (`enabled: false` by default), calls `.gald3r_sys/scripts/run_compliance_scan.ps1`, interprets exit codes (0=PASS continue, 1=WARN continue, 2=FAIL block), and gracefully skips when scanner is a stub. Created `.gald3r/config/COMPLIANCE_GATE.md` with gate configuration, prerequisites (T906 `g-skl-compliance`), and enable instructions. Requires 30-second timeout with abort-on-timeout behavior.

- **T898 â€” Harness Tuning Guide: AGENT_CONFIG.md** (2026-05-09): Created `.gald3r/config/AGENT_CONFIG.md` â€” central configuration for Gald3r agent harness performance. Documents five tunable knobs: `context_budget_tokens` (per-task-type recommendations: implementation 6kâ€“8k, review 4kâ€“5k, planning 8kâ€“10k, research 10kâ€“12k), `tool_call_order` (reads-first strategy), `max_retries` + `retry_backoff_seconds` (3 retries, exponential backoff), `temperature_by_task_type` (0.1 implementation, 0.2 review, 0.4 planning, 0.7 research), `memory_injection_timing` (preflight vs inline). Four named presets: `preset_implementation`, `preset_review`, `preset_planning`, `preset_research`. Per-task override mechanism via `agent_config_preset:` frontmatter field. Also includes `disable_version_check` and `version_feed_url` fields.

- **T891 â€” Maestro2 Harvest Specs: 2026 Tooling Update** (2026-05-09): Updated 7 Maestro2 task spec files with 2026 tooling implementation notes: T056 (Meshy 6 as primary 3D backend + Tripo 3.1 fallback + `Mesh3DProvider` abstraction), T057 (Trellis 2 architectural model fallback for room geometry), T060 (Voice-Pro as primary free TTS/voice cloning backend + `VoiceProvider` abstraction), T061 (Kimodo/Nvidia text-to-motion 6GB VRAM requirement + NanoBanana fallback), T063 (Kimodo for level editor character ambient motion), T054 (Persona Engine evaluation as Live2D rigging reference for 2D avatars), T069 (Hermes Agent Kanban dependency resolution algorithm as design study for K-002 topological sorting).

- **T889 â€” Failure-to-Skill Pipeline EVOLVE Operation** (2026-05-09): Added `### EVOLVE` operation to `g-skl-learn` SKILL.md across `.codex/`, `.claude/`, and `.cursor/` skill folders. -inspired pipeline: collect FAIL/PARTIAL_PASS rows from task Status History (minimum 2 failures), extract failure type + error patterns, cluster similar failures, synthesize proposed rule/skill amendments/preflight checks via LLM synthesis step, write proposals to `.gald3r/reports/evolve_proposals.md` for human review, apply approved proposals with provenance tracking. Constraints: minimum cluster size 2, max 5 proposals per run, human review required before apply.

- **T861 â€” Self-Healing CDP Helper Generation for Browser Skills** (2026-05-09): Added `## Self-Healing Error Recovery` section to `ui-control` SKILL.md across `.cursor/` and `.claude/` skill folders. Documents 4-step recovery pattern: detect failure (selector stale/404 route/invisible element), read page structure (snapshot, CDP commands), write targeted helper function using raw CDP/`page.evaluate()`, patch into live session and retry. Worked example for dynamic `data-testid` changes. Guidance on when to self-heal vs update selectors vs escalate to full spec update.

- **T848 â€” Higgsfield Maestro2 Animation Theme Pack Generation** (2026-05-09): Added `## Maestro2 Animation Theme Pack Generation` section to `higgsfield` SKILL.md across `.cursor/` and `.claude/` skill folders. Documents a 4-stage cloud-based creative pipeline using Higgsfield models (Seedance 2.0, Kling 2.0, Hailuo 02): concept generation â†’ style frames â†’ animation clips â†’ theme pack assembly. Includes output conventions, three example theme styles (Norse/Viking, Cyberpunk Neon, Minimal Glass Morphism) with palettes and example prompts, and cost guard (~120â€“200 credits per theme pack).

- **T847 â€” ComfyUI Agent Integration Skill** (2026-05-09): New `g-skl-comfyui` skill deployed to `.cursor/skills/` and `.claude/skills/`. Covers local GPU-accelerated image and video generation via ComfyUI V5: INSTALL (GPU check, ComfyUI V5 clone + setup), LAUNCH (server start, API readiness poll), RUN_WORKFLOW (JSON workflow submission, async queue polling, output retrieval), STATUS (server/queue health), STOP (process cleanup). Built-in workflow templates for SDXL text-to-image, AnimateDiff image-to-video, and Maestro2 theme starter. ComfyUI REST API reference, Maestro2 integration notes, and VRAM guardrails included.

- **T846 â€” Dynamic Instruction Assembly: g-skl-context-builder** (2026-05-09): New `g-skl-context-builder` skill deployed to `.cursor/skills/` and `.claude/skills/`. Builds token-budgeted context blocks dynamically from live `.gald3r/` state: BUILD (reads active tasks, active constraints, relevant subsystems, recent memory â†’ assembles priority-ordered context block within configurable token budget), INJECT (formats BUILD output for MCP compatibility), STATUS (reports available state and budget estimation). Integration with `g-go-code` and graceful degradation when components are missing.

- **T833 â€” gald3r In-App Version Check + Session-Start Update Notice** (2026-05-09): New `@g-update` command (`.cursor/commands/g-update.md` + `.claude/commands/g-update.md` parity) with `--check` (display current/latest versions), `--apply` (show per-install-type update instructions), and `--changelog` (display newer CHANGELOG entries since installed version). Optional non-blocking "Step 1.5: Version Check" added to `g-rl-25-gald3r_session_start.mdc` and `.claude/rules/g-rl-25-gald3r_session_start.md`. Respects `disable_version_check: true` in `AGENT_CONFIG.md` and a 3-second network timeout. `g-update` entry added to AGENTS.md commands table.

- **T626 â€” Maestro2 Architecture Reference Doc + Subsystem Spec Enrichment** (2026-05-09): Created comprehensive updated Maestro2 architecture reference document (`docs/20260509_125500_Cursor_MAESTRO2_ARCHITECTURE_REFERENCE.md`) superseding the prior May 1st doc with corrected counts and verified facts from T619â€“T625 deep dives (6-stage 3D pipeline not 5, NanoBanana = Gemini image model not animation format, 41 Meshy animation clips via `action_ids`, no ETag cache, 9 LLM providers not 7, 43 frontend pages, 249 components, 11 Zustand stores). Enriched 4 subsystem specs with "## Maestro2 Reference Implementation" sections: `voice-tts.md` (TTS sidecar, voice profile registry, gateway integration), `auth-security.md` (full JWT+OAuth+MFA+RBAC+API-key stack, `provider_key_service.py` AES-256-GCM pattern, `AUTH_DISABLED` warning), `communications.md` (Telegram/Discord/Twilio patterns, `dev_event_notifier.py` character-event routing), `streaming.md` (OBS WebSocket `obs_service.py`, scene structure, Stream Clean Mode, multi-platform RTMP, APScheduler stream scheduler). Subsystems `backend-api.md`, `agent-gateway.md`, `3d-pipeline.md`, `theme-engine.md`, `level-editor.md`, and `gald3r_throne_webview.md` were already enriched by T619â€“T625.

- **T903 â€” g-skl-security-scan: Two-Phase DeepSec Security Scanner** (2026-05-09): New `g-skl-security-scan` skill deployed across all 5 IDE skill folders (`.cursor/`, `.claude/`, `.agent/`, `.codex/`, `.opencode/`). Implements the Vercel DeepSec two-phase architecture: Phase 1 = fast regex surface discovery via ripgrep across 12 security pattern categories (hardcoded credentials, SQL injection, eval/exec, weak crypto, debug backdoors, path traversal, CORS wildcards, etc.) with no LLM calls; Phase 2 = parallel LLM analysis on flagged batches grouped by subsystem/type. Operations: `SCAN` (full two-phase), `FAST_SCAN` (Phase 1 regex only, free), `REPORT` (format existing report). Complements `g-skl-code-review` (general quality) with a security-specific deep scan. Cost guidance and `--estimate-only` mode included. Example run against `docker/` folder documented in skill.

- **T908 â€” g-skl-res-review: similarity_risk field for harvest provenance** (2026-05-09): Three-file update across all 5 IDE platforms. (1) `g-skl-res-review` SKILL.md gains mandatory `similarity_risk: low|medium|high|critical` field in every suggestion's output format, with an agent heuristic guide (match identifiers, algorithmic structure, >50% traceable â†’ `high`, verbatim unique strings â†’ `critical`); default is `medium`. Topology routing table updated to include `Sim. Risk` column. `## Summary` block added. (2) `g-skl-res-deep` SKILL.md Feature Catalog table gains `Sim. Risk` column (default `medium`). (3) `g-skl-res-apply` SKILL.md Step 1 gains Similarity Risk Pre-flight Check: prints risk summary on every run; blocks APPLY with â›” if any feature is `critical`; warns but continues for `high`. All 6 `g-res-apply` command files updated with a `## Similarity Risk Gate` section. Closes IP provenance gap identified in D101.

- **T926 â€” TurboVec Vector Compression Evaluation** (2026-05-09): ADR research document at `docs/20260509_Cursor_TURBOVEC_EVALUATION.md` evaluating Google TurboQuant / TurboVec as 8Ã— compression complement for gald3r_valhalla's pgvector backend. Decision: **DEFER** â€” library is alpha-stage, pgvector has no native INT8 distance operator (requires custom UDF), and current vault scale (~135K docs, ~800MB) does not mandate compression. Includes: pros/cons table, integration complexity breakdown, Python benchmark plan (recall@10 > 90% threshold), ~9-day implementation estimate, and re-evaluate triggers (vault > 2M docs, pgvector 0.8+, TurboVec v1.0 stable).

- **T880 â€” g-triage: External Backlog Intake Command** (2026-05-09): New `@g-triage` command (`.cursor/commands/g-triage.md` + `.claude/commands/g-triage.md` parity) that parses unstructured external input â€” emails, Slack dumps, meeting notes, pasted URLs â€” and routes each item to the correct gald3r destination. Five-phase workflow: (1) parse & classify input into items; (2) classify each as IDEA / BUG / TASK / INFO using keyword heuristics; (3) display structured triage table with confidence scores and proposed routing; (4) **hard-gated human approval** before any `.gald3r/` writes (approve all / approve N,M / reclassify / discard); (5) route approved items to `g-skl-ideas` CAPTURE, `g-skl-bugs` REPORT, or `g-skl-tasks` CREATE TASK. Urgency signals, bug signals, and idea signals documented. Related to `@g-idea-capture`, `@g-bug-add`, `@g-task-add`, and `@g-propose`.

- **T884 â€” g-skl-delegate: Engineering Team Delegation Workflow Skill** (2026-05-09): New `g-skl-delegate` skill deployed across all 5 IDE skill folders (`.cursor/`, `.claude/`, `.agent/`, `.codex/`, `.opencode/`) encoding delegation patterns for AI agent orchestration. Covers: (1) **Engineering team roles** â€” Planner / Coder / Reviewer / Coordinator mapped to `g-go`, `g-go-code`, `g-go-review`; (2) **Task brief template** â€” problem statement, context, constraints, out-of-scope, AC; (3) **Code review request template** â€” what to review, what to skip, review depth selector, LGTM success criteria; (4) **Quality gate checklists** â€” Feature / Bug Fix / Refactor variants with LGTM/FAIL verdict fields; (5) **Handoff protocol** â€” implementation â†’ review â†’ ship with explicit ownership transfer rules and Agent Notes format; (6) **Delegation anti-patterns** table â€” vague briefs, same-agent implement+review, missing skip lists. Aligns with existing `g-go` two-phase adversarial pipeline.

- **T887 â€” g-skl-cli-jcode: jcode Rust Coding Agent Platform Skill** (2026-05-09): New `g-skl-cli-jcode` platform skill deployed across all 5 IDE skill folders documenting jcode (MIT, Rust) as gald3r's low-overhead local agent runtime option. Performance comparison: 14ms startup vs 3.4s Claude Code (245Ã— faster), ~10 MB RAM per session, local embeddings via Ollama. Covers: installation via `cargo install jcode` or binary download; `~/.jcode/config.toml` config (model, embedding, session dir, ignore patterns); key flags (--headless, --session, --resume, --include, --embed-context); session management (list, resume, export, delete); Ollama model setup (qwen2.5-coder, deepseek-coder-v2, nomic-embed-text for embeddings); decision table (jcode vs Cursor vs Claude CLI vs Gemini CLI by scenario); gald3r integration patterns (task spec injection, jcode-as-coder + Cursor-as-coordinator pipeline, PowerShell batch runner, pre-commit hook); known caveats (no web access, no native `.gald3r/` support, context window varies by model).

- **T856 â€” file_index Plugin: Chunk-Level Search** (2026-05-09): `file_index` MCP plugin gains `action='search'` using `rg --json` to return structured code chunks `{path, line_start, line_end, match_line, snippet}` â€” 98% token savings vs read-whole-file. Includes 3-line context before/after each match, 50-chunk cap (configurable up to 200). Falls back to pure-Python grep when ripgrep unavailable. `grep` action gains `with_chunks=True` option for chunk-format output. Tree-sitter AST chunking evaluated per AC8 â€” ripgrep line-range chosen as sufficient for initial implementation (Tree-sitter deferred). File: `docker/gald3r/tools/plugins/file_index.py`.

- **T849** Persistent swarm dispatcher ADR: recommends gald3r_agent daemon (Option A); follow-up task T940 created (`gald3r_agent: Implement Persistent Swarm Dispatcher Daemon`). ADR at `.gald3r/reports/adr_persistent_swarm_dispatcher.md` documents crash-recovery via systemd/launchd/NSSM, WAKEUP_QUEUE.md session-boundary handoff, and HEARTBEAT.md heartbeat protocol.

- **T888 â€” g-skl-features CONSOLIDATE operation** (2026-05-09): New `CONSOLIDATE` operation added to `g-skl-features` skill across `.cursor/` and `.claude/` SKILL.md. Two-phase dedup workflow for harvest-heavy feature registries: `--scan` computes pairwise overlap scores (title keywords 50%, synonym detection 20%, harvest_sources 15%, subsystems 15%) across all `status: staging` feature files and outputs a ranked similarity report to `.gald3r/reports/consolidate_scan_YYYYMMDD.md`; `--apply` executes human-approved `[MERGE]` pairs by merging `## Collected Approaches`, unioning `harvest_sources:` and `subsystems:`, appending a `## Merge Log` to the canonical file, and marking retired files `status: archived` with redirect notes. Never deletes files; canonical = lower feat-NNN ID; only processes staging features.

- **T892 â€” OpenClaw platform recon** (2026-05-09): Research note at `docs/20260509_Cursor_OPENCLAW_PLATFORM_RECON.md` evaluating OpenClaw as gald3r's 7th platform candidate. Referenced by 8+ major AI agent repos (~250K stars). Assessment: **Partial / Unconfirmed** tier â€” system_prompt config likely supports always-apply rules but no native skill discovery path or slash-command namespace confirmed. Recommendation: defer `g-skl-platform-openclaw` creation until config file format confirms file-glob instructions support.

- **T855 â€” Multi-Client Tenant Isolation ADR** (2026-05-09): Architecture Decision Record at `docs/20260509_Cursor_MULTI_TENANT_ADR.md` evaluating three tenant isolation approaches for `gald3r_valhalla`. **Recommendation: Option B** â€” enforce `project_id` filters across all MCP plugins + add `project_id` to credentials table. Documents threat model; credential store identified as the highest-risk gap.

- **T904 â€” Symphony workflow.md pattern design** (2026-05-09): Design document at `docs/20260509_Cursor_SYMPHONY_WORKFLOW_MD_PATTERN.md` defining the optional `.gald3r/workflow.md` orchestration spec format. Documents Symphony vs gald3r comparison (gald3r advantage: native TASKS.md eliminates Linear.app dependency), schema, g-go-go (T533) integration path, and Ollama/local model substitution via `--model ollama://modelname`. `workflow.md` is explicitly optional â€” TASKS.md remains the source of truth.

- **T839 â€” PowerShell Hook Idempotency Guards**: Added `$env:GALD3R_HK_{HOOKNAME}_APPLIED` session-scoped environment variable guards to `g-hk-session-start.ps1`, `g-hk-vault-reindex.ps1`, `g-hk-vault-migrate.ps1`, and `g-hk-wrkspc-manifest-check.ps1` in both `.cursor/hooks/` and `.claude/hooks/`. Re-invoking these hooks in the same session now exits immediately with `[SKIP]`. All guards accept `-ForceRun` to bypass. Hooks that must always run (`g-hk-wpac-inbox-check.ps1`, `g-hk-pre-commit.ps1`, `g-hk-validate-shell.ps1`, `g-hk-pre-push.ps1`) are intentionally excluded. Pattern documented in `g-skl-platform-cursor` Section 11.

- **T844 â€” Pre-Flight Cost Confirmation Pattern**: New `## Cost-Guard Pattern` section in `skill-create` SKILL.md with the standard cost-estimate template, negotiate-down flow (offers cheaper alternatives when user hesitates), and checklist. Section 12 added to `g-skl-platform-cursor` SKILL.md (both `.cursor` and `.claude`). `higgsfield` SKILL.md updated with video generation negotiate-down flow (480pâ†’720p, 4sâ†’12s, cheaper model alternatives).

### Changed

- **T840 â€” vault_sync SHA1 Incremental Guard**: `vault_sync.py` `_content_hash()` now uses full SHA1 (40-char hex) instead of 16-char truncated SHA256. When content hash matches the stored value, `updated_at` (last_synced) is now touched via a lightweight `UPDATE` instead of returning silently unchanged. Migration note added to module docstring: `ALTER TABLE vault_notes ALTER COLUMN content_hash TYPE VARCHAR(40)`.

- **T853 â€” Claude Code Rate Limits Updated (May 2026)**: `g-skl-cli-claude` overnight/CI guidance updated to reflect doubled 5-hour rolling-window limits and removed peak-hour reduction for Pro/Max plans. Fact #50 added to `Learned Workspace Facts` in both `CLAUDE.md` and `AGENTS.md`. Previous "space large batches" guidance relaxed accordingly.

- **T860 â€” g-skl-browser-use: Production Browser Harness Skill** (2026-05-09): New `g-skl-browser-use` skill wrapping the `browser-use` library (YC W25, $17M seed) as gald3r's production browser automation layer. Deployed across all 5 IDE skill folders (`.cursor/`, `.claude/`, `.agent/`, `.codex/`, `.opencode/`) with byte-identical parity. Covers: decision table contrasting with `ui-control` (dev/test vs production/agentic); installation (`pip install browser-use` + `playwright install chromium`); auth pattern (persistent Chrome profile via `--remote-debugging-port` + `--user-data-dir`, `connect_over_cdp` inherit-session pattern); self-healing CDP pattern (agent reads helper file â†’ writes missing function â†’ patches live session â†’ retries); BUX cloud tier (persistent profiles, 195-country residential proxies, CAPTCHA solving, stealth fingerprinting, free tier); security warnings (domain allow-list, credential isolation, sandboxed helper file path, gald3r permission hook integration, rate limiting, ToS compliance); complete worked example â€” competitor pricing monitor (login-required, anti-bot) that extracts pricing table, diffs against last snapshot, and writes a vault note to `research/competitive/`.

- **T923** g-migrate command: automated API/skill interface migration across callers (`.cursor/commands/g-migrate.md`, all platforms) â€” closes the "skill upgrade breaks callers" problem

- **T850 â€” Cross-Agent Durable Task Memory: Agent Notes section** (2026-05-09): Task file format gains an optional `## Agent Notes` section â€” a lightweight, append-only handoff surface for parallel and sequential agent sessions. Format: `[AGENT:{platform}-{role}] [ISO-8601 timestamp] Note content`. New `WRITE_NOTES` operation added to `g-skl-tasks` (both `.cursor` and `.claude` SKILL.md) with PowerShell append pattern and rules (append-only, survive worktree cleanup, read by `g-go` coordinator on claim). `AGENTS.md` Task File Format section updated with the new section template and behavioral description. Addresses the "researcher drops notes, writer picks them up" cross-session handoff pattern.

- **T851 â€” Skill Marketplace: Community Skill/Agent Sharing Design** (2026-05-09): Architecture design proposal at `docs/20260509_Cursor_SKILL_MARKETPLACE_DESIGN.md`. Proposes GitHub Releases as distribution backend, `index.yaml` catalog format with skill metadata, `@g-skill-install`/`@g-skill-publish`/`@g-skill-list`/`@g-skill-update` command surface, security review requirements, SemVer versioning, and seed catalog with 5 existing skill packs. Positions gald3r ahead of Hermes v0.14 community agent pool.

- **T852 â€” Webhook Triggers: Event-Driven Agent Wake-Up Design** (2026-05-09): Architecture design proposal at `docs/20260509_Cursor_WEBHOOK_TRIGGERS_DESIGN.md`. Designs `POST /v1/webhook/{project_id}/{event_type}` endpoint for `gald3r_valhalla` with HMAC-SHA256 secret validation, `webhook_triggers.yaml` config format, WAKEUP_QUEUE.md integration, `@g-webhook-register` command, security model, and integration path with Anthropic's May 2026 webhook announcement.

- **T876 â€” Auto-Evolving Session Learning Extraction Loop** (2026-05-09): `g-go-code` and `g-go-review` now automatically extract architectural decisions and patterns into `.gald3r/learned-facts.md` after each task completes â€” no manual `/g-learn` required. **g-go-code** gains a new **Step 5a "Auto-Learn Extraction"** that runs after the docs check for every task moved to `[ðŸ”]`: reads the task's `## Status History` + implementation notes, produces 0â€“3 candidate facts, deduplicates against existing entries (case-insensitive substring match, first 80 chars), appends novel facts as `- [YYYY-MM-DD] {fact} (context: T{task_id})`, reports `ðŸ§  {N} new fact(s) learned` in the handoff summary, and optionally calls `memory_capture_session` when the MCP backend is available. **g-go-review** gains a new **Step g) "Auto-Learn Extraction"** after the docs check that fires on PASS verdicts (extracts verified patterns) and on `[ðŸš¨]` items (failure-trajectory learning: "T{id} reached [ðŸš¨] after N review attempts. Recurring failure: ..."). **g-skl-learn** SKILL.md updated with an expanded `## Session Integration` section documenting the T876 auto-extraction behavior and confirming that the manual `/g-learn` command is unchanged. Both `.cursor` and `.claude` surfaces updated (full parity).



- **T906 â€” g-skl-compliance: Code Compliance Skill and Commands** (2026-05-09): New `g-skl-compliance` skill (full + adv tiers) wrapping ORT, FOSSA CLI, Snyk, PMD CPD, and a zero-dependency manifest-parse fallback behind a unified gald3r compliance interface. Four operations: `SCAN` (auto-detects best available scanner via priority chain ortâ†’fossaâ†’snykâ†’pmdâ†’fallback, writes `.gald3r/reports/compliance_YYYYMMDD.md`), `REPORT` (displays last scan result), `GATE` (returns exit-code verdict: 0=PASS/1=WARN/2=FAIL for pre-push hook consumption), `STATUS` (shows which scanners are on `$PATH` with auth status). Fallback mode parses `package.json`, `pyproject.toml`, `Cargo.toml`, `go.mod`, `pom.xml`, and `*.gemspec` for declared licenses using a canonical risk table (GPL/AGPL/SSPLâ†’`block`; LGPL/MPL/CDDLâ†’`warn`; MIT/Apache-2.0/BSD/ISC/0BSDâ†’`ok`; unknownâ†’`warn`). Three companion commands (`@g-compliance-scan`, `@g-compliance-report`, `@g-compliance-gate`) deployed across all 6 IDE platforms (`.cursor`/`.claude`/`.agent`/`.codex`/`.opencode`/`.copilot`). SKILL.md deployed across all 5 skill-capable platforms with byte-identical MD5 parity (`B03920C28C419893DC2604FA696662FF`). Reference docs `license_risk_table.md` and `scanner_setup.md` included in skill `reference/` folder. PowerShell helper stub `.gald3r_sys/scripts/run_compliance_scan.ps1` with `TODO[TASK-906â†’TASK-<follow-up>]` annotation for full pipeline implementation. SKILL_INDEX.md regenerated via `.gald3r_sys/skills/g-skl-setup/scripts/generate_skill_index.ps1 -Apply` across all 5 skill-capable platforms. Feeds T907 (`g-git-push` compliance gate hook) and T908 (`g-skl-res-review` similarity risk field).

- **T838 â€” g-go Coordinator: Pure Routing Orchestrator Refactor** (2026-05-09): `g-go` coordinator skill (`g-go.md` across `.cursor/` and `.claude/`) now explicitly enforces the **routing-only mandate** â€” "the coordinator never implements; it only routes, observes, and reconciles." - **T836 â€” g-go-code Mid-Task Checkpoint Self-Evaluation** (2026-05-09): Added mandatory mid-session checkpoint mechanism to `g-go-code` (`.cursor` and `.claude` command files). Mirrors the Hermes v0.12 checkpoint pattern (Strategic Feature SF-4) with full task-file provenance and gald3r AC-awareness.

Output is a structured `âœ… PASS / âš ï¸ WARN / âŒ FAIL` report with a one-line `ðŸ’¡` fix hint per check. `--fix` flag applies a narrow safe auto-fix scope (create missing directories, stub `.identity` when absent) â€” routing, credentials, and connection settings are explicitly never touched (the OpenClaw 5.5 lesson). - **T879 â€” Manus Brain Planning Gate in g-go-code** (2026-05-09): Added mandatory `Step 0: Generate Locked Implementation Plan` to `g-go-code` across both `.cursor/commands/g-go-code.md` and `.claude/commands/g-go-code.md`. - **T877 â€” g-propose: One-Shot Proposal Generation Command** (2026-05-09): New `@g-propose` command (`.cursor/commands/g-propose.md` + parity across `.claude`, `.agent`, `.codex`, `.opencode`, `.copilot`) that generates a complete proposal package from a short description in a single invocation. Accepts `"feature description"` plus optional `--scope` and `--constraints` flags. Produces `docs/proposals/YYYYMMDD_HHMMSS_Cursor_PROPOSAL_<slug>.md` containing: Executive Summary, Problem Statement, Proposed Solution, Technical Design (architecture / data model / API surface / dependencies), Acceptance Criteria (paste-ready for task specs), a pre-filled PRD Draft (paste-ready for `@g-prd-add`), a 3â€“7 task breakdown table (paste-ready for `@g-task-add`), Risks & Alternatives, and Open Questions. No `.gald3r/` writes occur until the human explicitly approves â€” the proposal is staged for review first. After generation, the command shows a summary and a three-option next-step menu: Approve (run `@g-prd-add` + `@g-task-add`), Refine (edit proposal file), or Discard. Optional `--from-file` mode re-reads a refined proposal and outputs the approval commands without regenerating. Bridges the gap between raw idea and actionable spec without requiring separate invocations of `@g-plan`, `@g-prd-add`, and `@g-task-add`.

### Fixed

- **BUG-050 â€” T600 hook system shipped 3 BOM-less PS files with smart punctuation** (gald3r_dev source-only, `g-go-go` autopilot ITER 8 2026-05-06): same regression class as BUG-016 / BUG-041 / BUG-049. Detected by ITER 8 fresh-reviewer: `scripts/gald3r_worktree.ps1`, `.claude/hooks/g-hk-http-event.ps1`, and `.claude/hooks/g-hk-pre-commit.ps1` were authored as UTF-8 without BOM and contained em-dashes (U+2014) and section signs (U+00A7), causing Windows PowerShell 5.1 `ParseFile` to fail with "missing string terminator" because the multi-byte sequences land inside double-quoted strings on the default ANSI codepage. `gald3r_worktree.ps1` is the active worktree primitive used by every `g-go*` swarm flow on Windows; the regression would have bricked `g-go-code` / `g-go --swarm` / `g-go-go` on stock Windows hosts. Fixed in same commit by re-saving all 3 files as UTF-8 *with* BOM. Parse-clean reverified in PowerShell 5.1 + 7; helper self-test 14/14 still PASS. Per-script BOM verification recorded in commit body.

- **T531 â€” `g-go*` Gald3r Housekeeping Commit Gate**: New controller-only gate sits between the **WPAC inbox Gate** and the **Clean Controller Gate** on all six `g-go*` paths. Runs at two points: (a) **preflight** â€” before claims, worktrees, coding, review, or swarm partitioning; and (b) **post-coordinator-write** â€” immediately after coordinator-owned shared `.gald3r/` writes (task/bug status updates, review-result writes, sent_orders ledger updates, safe report/log outputs) and before the next major phase. New helper `.gald3r_sys/skills/g-skl-git-commit/scripts/gald3r_housekeeping_commit.ps1` reads `git status --porcelain=v1 -uall`, classifies dirty paths against an explicit allowlist (TASKS.md, BUGS.md, FEATURES.md, PRDS.md, SUBSYSTEMS.md, IDEA_BOARD.md, learned-facts.md, tasks/**, bugs/**, features/**, prds/**, subsystems/**, reports/**, logs/pcac_auto_actions.log, workspace/sent_orders/**, workspace/inbox.md) and a deny list (.identity, .user_id, .project_id, .vault_location, vault/**, config/**, .gald3r-worktree.json, secret-named files), and returns one of `clean`, `safe-gald3r-housekeeping`, `safe-gald3r-coordination`, `unsafe-gald3r`, `mixed-dirty`, `conflict`, `drift-detected`, `committed-*`, or `config-fault`. When dirty paths are exclusively safe controller `.gald3r/` housekeeping, `-Apply` stages **only** classified-safe paths via explicit `git add -- <paths>` (never `git add .`), re-checks for drift, and creates a focused `chore(gald3r): preflight gald3r housekeeping` (preflight) or `chore(gald3r): commit g-go coordination state` (post-write) commit with optional `Task: #<id>` / `Bug: BUG-<id>` body. Unsafe / mixed / conflict / drift / unknown / member-repo-target â†’ preserves the existing Clean Controller Gate hard-block. Member-repo targets (marker-only `.gald3r/` with `.identity` but no manifest and no `TASKS.md`) are refused with `config-fault`; the helper never writes member repository `.gald3r/` content. New fixture-based test `scripts/tests/test_gald3r_housekeeping_commit.ps1` covers 11 cases (clean / safe-housekeeping / nested safe / mixed-dirty / unsafe identity / unsafe config / unknown path / source-only / apply-commits / post-write classify / member-repo refusal). Rule update lands in `g-rl-33-enforcement_catchall` and propagates across `.cursor/`, `.claude/`, `.agent/`, `.codex/`, `.opencode/`. Command updates land in all six `g-go*` files across `.cursor/`, `.claude/`, `.agent/`, `.codex/`, `.opencode/`, `.copilot/`. Controller-only behavior; member-repo marker-only `.gald3r/` policy unchanged.

### Changed

- **g-medic active-index, dry-run, output, and PCAC-scope contracts**: `g-skl-medic` now explicitly scopes task orphan/phantom checks to active `TASKS.md` rows and direct child `.gald3r/tasks/task*.md` files only, and the task-row parser contract now requires both bullet rows (`- [âœ…] **Task 090**: ...`) and table rows (`| [âœ…] | [090](tasks/task090_*.md) | ... |`) to be normalized and deduplicated before counts are reported. Archive, backup, imported, quarantine, and historical task subfolders must be reported separately with source metadata, preventing medic from counting harvested/archive files as hundreds of active orphan tasks. The skill and command wrappers also clarify that L1 auto-apply is disabled under `--dry-run`, ordinary L1-L4 dry-runs must not write report/backlog/status files, material findings must be shown in full rather than hidden behind short summaries, and WPAC inbox hooks run only when the project is actually a WPAC participant rather than merely a Workspace-Control owner.
- **g-medic L4 Workspace-Control split**: `g-skl-medic` now treats Workspace-Control and PCAC as separate L4 coordination surfaces. Disabling PCAC skips only WPAC topology/inbox checks; L4 still runs Workspace-Control manifest, member reachability, git status, routing policy, and marker-only diagnostics when `.gald3r/workspace/workspace_manifest.yaml` is active.
- **BUG-037 / T800 â€” g-medic curate dry-run recommendations**: `.gald3r_sys/skills/g-skl-medic/scripts/gald3r_medic_curate.ps1` now generates a first-use readable curation report with an executive summary, suggested first batch, `index_candidates`, and non-binding `suggested_moves` (source, target, risk, confidence, rationale). The applyable top-level `moves` array stays empty until an approved reviewer copies entries into it, preserving the explicit `-Apply -ProposalJson` safety gate. Feature file counting now recognizes both `featNNN` and `feat-NNN` naming styles.
- **T508**: Retired stale paid-crawler guidance from crawl-related skills and MCP documentation; `g-skl-platform-crawl`, recon docs, platform-doc RAG descriptions, and Docker/env docs now standardize on the crawl4ai crawl path.
- **PLAN.md**: Realigned Current Focus and Build Order with the full workspace (external `gald3r_template_*`, Workspace-Control manifest and marker-only members, Valhalla MCP/backend boundary per Task 177, MCP tool-layer doc + T483-T493 ladder, gald3r_throne and gald3r_agent tracks, adopted gald3r_web tasks, verification queue); updated PRD index for completed work; added cross-cutting initiative table and 2026-05-01 phase-history entry.
- **T495 / T496 ï¿½ blast-radius clean gates**: `g-rl-33`, all `g-go*` commands, GitHub Copilot prompts, `g-skl-workspace`, and **README.md** now extend the Clean Controller / Pre-Reconciliation gates to **every git root in the computed touch set** ï¿½ always the orchestration checkout; plus manifest-resolved roots for task/bug `workspace_repos:` (v1); optionally `extended_touch_repos:`, swarm `touch_repos:` handoffs, and subsystem `locations:` absolute paths (v2). Still **no** blanket requirement that every workspace manifest member be clean on every run.

### Fixed

- **T494 / BUG-027 (gald3r_throne)**: Fixed left-side navigation links going dead after a project is loaded. Root cause: `Shell.tsx` updated `activeSection` state on left-nav button clicks but the `<main>` content branched only on `phase` (`picker | loading | dashboard | error`); `Dashboard` never consulted `activeSection`, so once `phase === 'dashboard'` clicking left-nav buttons moved only the visual highlight while the rendered panel set never changed. Secondary contributor: `App.css` `.shell__nav-item { cursor: default }` made the buttons feel non-interactive. **Fix** (member-only, `gald3r_throne` only): (1) `Dashboard.tsx` now accepts `activeSection: keyof Strings['sections']` and routes panel rendering through a `switch` â€” `section.workspace` keeps the full overview (no regression on the default landing); `section.project` shows identity + project; `section.tasks` shows tasks; `section.bugs` shows bugs; `section.features` / `section.releases` / `section.subsystems` / `section.plans` / `section.vault` / `section.settings` render empty-state placeholders sourced from `src/strings/empty_states.json` so every left-nav button opens an intelligible view. (2) `Shell.tsx` passes `activeSection` to `Dashboard`. (3) `App.css` `.shell__nav-item { cursor: pointer }` plus a non-active `:hover` rule. Project context (`phase.summary`) is preserved across section navigation â€” clicking a left-nav button only updates `activeSection`; `phase` stays `dashboard` with the loaded summary intact. Member `.gald3r/` invariant respected â€” only `gald3r_throne/src/**` files touched. Delivered by `g-go --swarm tasks 494` single-mode auto-downgrade (sole runnable item in queue).

- **T216**: Workspace-Control populated-gald3r-project **active-vs-terminal artifact import policy** landed. New design doc at `docs/20260428_165201_Claude_GALD3R_ADOPTION_IMPORT_POLICY.md` (`spec_version: "1.0"`) is the policy companion to the T215 ID-mapping/provenance schema and the T214 `populated_gald3r_adoption` mode. Specifies, for the 19-area discovery inventory from T214, the per-artifact-type lifecycle classification rules that decide whether each source artifact becomes `active-control-visible` (full record copied; rendered in controller `TASKS.md`/`BUGS.md`/`FEATURES.md`/`PRDS.md`/`RELEASES.md`/`CONSTRAINTS.md`/`IDEA_BOARD.md` with `[adopted:{member_id}]` prefix), `merge-candidate` (surfaced in dry-run plan; never auto-applied; requires `--accept-merge` / `--skip-merge`), `archived-reference` (routed through T204 archive buckets with `Adopted From` column extension), `link-only` (reference stub at `.gald3r/adopted/{member_id}/{kind}/{name}.ref`; bytes never copied), or `conflict-deferred` (apply REFUSES until explicit decision). **39-row master import policy matrix** in ï¿½6 covers every (artifact-type ï¿½ source-status) combination across 19 T214 inventory areas. **Per-artifact-type rules** (ï¿½1.1?ï¿½1.17): tasks/bugs/subtasks (active ? active-control-visible; terminal ? archived-reference; orphaned subtasks rendered under synthetic `[adopted-orphan:{member_id}:{parent_source_id}]` header); features (T084 staging lifecycle: `staging`/`specced` ? active, `committed` ? merge-candidate, `shipped`/`deferred`/`superseded` ? archived-reference); PRDs (T169/C-019 freeze-aware: `draft`/`review`/`approved`/`in-implementation` ? active, `released`/`superseded` ? conflict-deferred with explicit `--resolve-conflict prd-{id}=mirror|link|skip` decisions, `archived` ? archived-reference); releases (`assigned_tasks` rewritten via T215 ID map, `roadmap_visibility` from T052 preserved); constraints (T120 `scope:` preserved; auto-expired ? archived-reference; otherwise merge-candidate; title suffixed `(adopted from {member_id})`); subsystems (no overlap ? link-only namespaced as `{name}-{member_id}`; exact name match ? conflict-deferred with `keep-source`/`keep-controller`/`merge`/`skip`; fuzzy match Levenshtein ? 2 ? merge-candidate); plan/mission/identity (always link-only ? source-anchored); ideas (per-row classification with synthetic `idea-{member_id}-{seq}` IDs); linking/PCAC (link-only; source-side `workspace_manifest.yaml` triggers conflict-deferred unless `--accept-source-controller-as-data-only`); reports (link-only default; `--copy-reports {pattern}` opt-in to archived-reference for SWOT/KPI capture); logs (always link-only; bytes never copied); experiments (active ? merge-candidate; terminal ? archived-reference under `.gald3r/archive/adopted/{member_id}/experiments/`); source's existing archive sub-trees (preserved verbatim under `.gald3r/archive/adopted/{member_id}/{tasks|bugs}/{source_range}/` ? NOT re-bucketed into controller ordinals; T215 collision #9); specifications collection + learned facts (link-only); unknown / custom folders (`conflict-deferred` by default; apply REFUSES until `--accept-unknown {pattern} as {class}` or `--reject-unknown {pattern}`). **Active index rendering rules** (ï¿½2): 8 distinct rendering specs covering `[adopted:{member_id}]` prefix injection, PCAC + adoption stack (`[WPAC] [adopted:{member_id}] {title}`), subsystems list rewrite via per-adoption ID map, mandatory `<!-- ADOPTION PROVENANCE -->` markdown footer on every adopted active controller-side file. **Dependency remapping** (ï¿½3): two new frontmatter fields `source_dependencies` (original source IDs preserved verbatim) and `unresolved_source_dependencies` (deps with no controller mapping) land on adopted active tasks/features/PRDs; three-way mapping handles active-active (standard ID rewrite), active-archived (T212 `requires_verified_dependencies` semantics: archived = passed verification ? satisfies dep), and missing (drops from `dependencies:`, surfaces in `unresolved_source_dependencies`). **Terminal routing** (ï¿½4): adopted terminal artifacts use controller's ordinal bucket sequence per T204; source numeric ID preserved in `archive.original_task_id`/`archive.original_bug_id`; source's own archive sub-tree preserved verbatim in parallel namespace; `archive_{tasks|bugs}_{range}.md` index files gain backward-compatible `Adopted From` column (`{member_id}:source-task-NNN`; `?` for non-adoption rows); immutable historical lookup invariants honored. **Conflict resolution vocabulary** (ï¿½5): 6 explicit decisions (`keep-source`/`keep-controller`/`merge`/`skip`/`mirror`/`link`); apply CLI extends `@g-wrkspc-adopt --apply --plan {report-path}` with `--resolve-conflict {kind}-{id}={decision}`, `--accept-merge {kind}={id} as {class}`, `--skip-merge {kind}={id}`, `--accept-unknown {pattern} as {class}`, `--reject-unknown {pattern}`, `--copy-reports {pattern}`, `--shipped-features-as-link-only`, `--accept-source-controller-as-data-only`; **no silent defaults** ? every conflict-deferred item requires an explicit decision before apply proceeds. **Worked examples** (ï¿½8): 7 traceability scenarios covering active task with active-task dep, released PRD with `mirror` resolution, subsystem name collision, unknown folder handling, terminal task ? - **T212**: Nonblocking rolling swarm pipeline policy added. `@g-go-code`, `@g-go-code-swarm`, `@g-go`, and `@g-go-swarm` now treat code-complete checkpoint commits as stable handoff points rather than global stop signs: checkpointed awaiting-verification dependencies count as implementation-satisfied for downstream coding unless a task opts into `requires_verified_dependencies: true`. Review remains mandatory and runs from committed checkpoints in a parallel lane; review failures requeue the failed item and any downstream checkpoint consumers while unrelated implementation waves continue. `g-skl-tasks` now documents the optional `requires_verified_dependencies` frontmatter field and sprint planning semantics for rolling pipelines.
- **T212 follow-up**: Implementation-only command boundaries clarified. `@g-go-code` and `@g-go-code-swarm` now explicitly forbid spawning reviewer agents, `@g-go-review`, `@g-go-review-swarm`, `gald3r-code-reviewer`, or full adversarial review subagents. Code mode may run only smoke/unit readiness gates such as import/build/typecheck/lint, focused tests, acceptance-criteria self-checks, workspace/constraint gates, stub/TODO checks, and bug-discovery checks. Full review remains isolated to `@g-go`, `@g-go-swarm`, `@g-go-review`, and `@g-go-review-swarm`.

### Changed
- **T222 / T225**: Restored `gald3r_dev` self-hosting parity as an explicit maintainer path and narrowed Workspace-Control dirty-state blocking. `scripts/platform_parity_sync.ps1 -SelfHostingRootSource` now uses root `.cursor/` as the source for root platform folders plus `G:/gald3r_ecosystem/gald3r_template_adv/`, then runs `tier_sync.ps1` for `G:/gald3r_ecosystem/gald3r_template_full/` and `G:/gald3r_ecosystem/gald3r_template_slim/`; root-only maintainer tooling remains excluded from template targets. `scripts/workspace_template_export.py` now blocks dirty member repos only when dirty paths overlap planned writes, while unrelated dirty entries are reported as advisory.

- **T209**: `g-go-code-swarm` and `g-go-swarm` now auto-downgrade to standard single-agent implementation when exactly one runnable item remains after Workspace-Control preflight, while preserving hard blockers for unknown workspace members, non-git-root targets, and unauthorized member writes.
- **T208**: Review finalization now creates a coordinator-owned review-result commit after PASS or FAIL status writes by default. `g-go-review`, `g-go-review --swarm`, and `g-go` Phase 2 commit verified `[?]`, failed `[??]`, requires-user-attention `[??]`, and mixed verdict states unless a narrow repository safety blocker prevents a safe commit; final staging remains explicit-path only.
- **T207**: Default implementation-to-review handoff now creates a code-complete checkpoint commit before review. `g-go-code` / `g-go --swarm` coordinators record the checkpoint branch/SHA after final shared writes, and `g-go-review` / `g-go-review --swarm` use that committed source for clean `review` / `review-swarm` worktrees by default. Dirty snapshot review remains available only as an explicit fallback for uncommitted or non-branch-addressable sources.
- **T206**: Swarm reconciliation policy hardened for `g-go --swarm`, `g-go-code --swarm`, and `g-go-review --swarm`. Bucket agents now operate as handoff producers that return patches/artifacts/evidence and proposed status rows; the coordinator alone writes shared `.gald3r` status/index files, changelog/docs updates, generated Copilot prompts, parity sync output, final staging, and commits. Swarm guidance now forbids `git add .` in bucket worktrees and requires explicit path staging that excludes `.gald3r-worktree.json`, ownership metadata, terminal transcripts, logs, and other non-deliverable artifacts.
- **T167**: WPAC sends are now atomic, never queued, never task-creating ? the `.gald3r/workspace/sent_orders/order_*.md` ledger is the only outbound tracking surface (status: `sent` ? `acknowledged` ? `in-progress` ? `completed` | `blocked` | `abandoned`, where `abandoned` is a new status added for stale-order closure); `g-skl-wpac-order` no longer creates a local broadcast tracker task; `g-skl-wpac-ask` no longer creates a `[Waiting]` blocked task and instead records a `type: ask` entry in the sent_orders ledger with optional `cross_project_ref:` linkage on the local task that depends on the parent action; `g-skl-wpac-notify` and `g-skl-wpac-sync` reaffirm fire-and-forget semantics (no tracker task, no ledger entry for notify); `g-skl-tasks` CREATE TASK rejects task titles matching `^Send (PCAC|order|broadcast|notify|ask|sync) to`, `await.*responses?.*(child|children|peer|sibling)`, or `^PCAC\s+(send|broadcast|notify|order|ask)` with the message "Use sent_orders ledger, not a task"; `g-rl-25` Step 6b adds stale-order detection (>30d in `sent`/`acknowledged`) with `@g-wpac-status --close <ord-id>` formal-abandon flow; `g-rl-33` documents both anti-patterns. Migration report at `.gald3r/reports/pcac_task_migration_2026-04-25.md` confirms zero legacy await/tracker tasks exist in this project.
- **T172**: `g-go-review`, `g-go-review-swarm`, and `g-go` Phase 2 now document review-side isolation: claimed review items use a T170 `review` / `review-swarm` worktree when branch-addressable, fall back to read-only snapshot mode for uncommitted checkout/worktree sources, record review isolation metadata, preserve active implementation worktrees, and keep swarm review writes coordinator-owned.
- **T171**: `g-go-code`, `g-go`, `g-go-code-swarm`, and `g-go-swarm` coding workflows now consume the T170 worktree primitive before implementation edits; single-agent runs record worktree claim metadata, swarm coordinators allocate one coding worktree per bucket, bucket agents run from assigned worktrees, and coordinators reconcile bucket outputs before final task/bug status writes.
- **T188**: Workspace-Control export hygiene review resolved bootstrap blockers by replacing concrete `gald3r_dev` absolute-path examples in installable PCAC/tier/memory template content with generic placeholders and narrowing `scripts/workspace_template_export.py` secret-literal scanning so intentional `g-skl-code-review` security reference examples are classified as documentation rather than export leaks.
- **T185**: Workspace-Control git/worktree boundaries now require every manifest repository to be treated as an independent git root with separate status, branch, remotes, rollback, and worktree context; `g-skl-workspace`, workspace commands/prompts, git sanity, commit guidance, README/AGENTS/CLAUDE docs, `.gald3r/workspace/workspace_manifest.yaml`, and `scripts/workspace_template_export.py` now report or enforce per-repo boundaries and member-ID branch/worktree naming for multi-repo work.
- **T182**: Workspace-Control enforcement tightened across `g-skl-workspace`, `g-skl-tasks`, `g-skl-bugs`, `g-go`, `g-go-code`, `g-go-review`, `g-git-sanity`, and `g-skl-git-commit`; routing metadata now validates against `.gald3r/workspace/workspace_manifest.yaml`, omitted metadata remains current-repo-only, unknown member IDs block when a manifest exists, member writes require explicit `workspace_repos` plus compatible `workspace_touch_policy` and manifest permission, and scope-widening updates require Status History context.

### Fixed
- **BUG-012**: `g-skl-wpac-spawn` did not scaffold `.gitignore` or `opencode.json` into spawned projects ? new projects were git-committing `.gald3r/` data and invisible to OpenCode IDE. Fixed by adding `.gitignore` and `opencode.json` to Step 3 of `g-skl-wpac-spawn` scaffold flow, with inline fallback defaults when template source is missing; pre-flight check updated; 10-target MD5 parity verified.
- **BUG-017**: `scripts/gald3r_worktree.ps1` aborted on git's stderr `Preparing worktree` progress line under PowerShell 7+ ? `$ErrorActionPreference = "Stop"` plus `2>&1` merged stream wraps stderr lines as `ErrorRecord` items that terminate the pipeline before `$LASTEXITCODE` is checked. `Invoke-Git` now scopes `$ErrorActionPreference = "Continue"` around the git call (saved/restored in `try`/`finally`) and converts merged-stream `ErrorRecord` items to plain strings so progress lines pass through and `$LASTEXITCODE` remains the only failure signal; real failures still throw with git's full stderr text. Unblocks every swarm pipeline (`g-go`, `g-go-code`, `g-go-review`, all `--swarm` variants) and Task 170/171/172 isolation contracts. Propagated across all 21 copies (1 root canonical + 20 IDE/template skill mirrors); positive + negative repro tests both pass.

Phase 2 watcher script + `@g-vault-process-inbox` command ? `raw-inbox-watcher.ps1` (300+ lines, manual-trigger only) scans `{vault}/raw/` and routes drops rules-based: `*.md` ? `research/articles/`, single URL `*.txt` ? `g-skl-ingest-url`, single YouTube URL `*.txt` ? `g-skl-ingest-youtube` (`fetch_transcript.py`), multi-line text `*.txt` ? wrapped `.md` with article frontmatter to `research/articles/`, `*.pdf`/`*.png`/`*.jpg` ? deferred to Phase 3 (move to `raw/failed/` with stub note). ### Fixed
- **BUG-007 (via T113)**: All `vault_*` MCP plugins returned `"Database not configured"` since 2026-04-05 because `RAGDatabase.__init__` raised when Postgres was still booting at container start, leaving `db = None` for the lifetime of the container. `RAGDatabase` is now resilient: `__init__` no longer raises on transient pool failure, and `get_connection()` lazily retries `_init_pool()` on first use so the system self-heals once Postgres is reachable. `server.py` also constructs a `RAGDatabase` shell even after a pool init error so plugins return useful errors instead of the generic "Database not configured" message. Verified: `vault_list` returned 1,441 notes, `vault_search` returned semantic matches, container log shows `db=connected`. Restored 7 vault tools + memory + RAG.
- **BUG-008 (inline during T113)**: `docker/Dockerfile` `COPY templates/ ./templates/` was broken since the repo restructure to `G:/gald3r_ecosystem/gald3r_template_full/` / `G:/gald3r_ecosystem/gald3r_template_slim/` / `G:/gald3r_ecosystem/gald3r_template_adv/`. Updated Dockerfile to copy `G:/gald3r_ecosystem/gald3r_template_full/` and updated `.dockerignore` to whitelist `G:/gald3r_ecosystem/gald3r_template_full/` instead of the missing `templates/`. Container path `/app/templates/` preserved so `install_rest` did not need changes.
- **BUG-009 (inline during T091)**: `docker/gald3r/tools/plugins/vault_export.py` UPDATE statement marked notes as exported via `id = ANY(%s)`, which psycopg2 sent as `text[]` against a `uuid` column ? Postgres rejected with `operator does not exist: uuid = text`. Cast the parameter as `id = ANY(%s::uuid[])` and explicitly `str()`-converted each id to make intent unambiguous. The whole `vault_export` tool was effectively unusable with the default `mark_exported=true` until this fix.
- **BUG-011**: `g-skl-ingest-youtube/scripts/fetch_transcript.py` (7806 bytes, MD5 `96936D11?`) was missing from 17 of 20 IDE targets ? only the three `.cursor` template trees had it. Discovered while implementing T111 (raw-inbox watcher needed the script for YouTube URL drops). The recommended fix in the bug record (`platform_parity_sync.ps1 -Sync`) was confirmed inert: the parity script only checks **skill-directory** presence (line 195: `if ($name -notin $targetSkills)`), not skill subfolder contents ? every target had the `g-skl-ingest-youtube/` directory and its `SKILL.md`, so the script reported zero gaps. Resolved by direct PowerShell `Copy-Item` to all 17 missing targets; final state **20/20 MD5 parity** verified. Watcher `BUG[BUG-011]` annotation removed and re-propagated; `G:/gald3r_ecosystem/gald3r_template_full/` fallback retained as defense-in-depth. Live-verified end-to-end: real-run watcher with YouTube URL fixture resolved through root `.cursor/` and produced a transcript note in `vault/research/videos/`. Second-order limitation (parity-script-no-recursion) logged in `multiple-ide-platform-parity` activity log + decision D064 as a candidate for future improvement.
- **BUG-010 (inline during T091)**: `vault_notes.exported_at` column was missing from existing-volume databases ? `13_vault_notes.sql` declares it for fresh init, but Postgres only runs `init_db/*.sql` on first volume initialization (knowledge fact #21), so older volumes never received it. Added idempotent migration `docker/init_db/15_vault_notes_exported_at.sql` (`ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS` + partial index on `exported_at IS NULL`) and applied to the live DB via `docker exec` per knowledge fact #22. `vault_export` now succeeds end-to-end: returned `success: true, exported_count: 1` for the lone DB-resident video note.
- **T091**: Video research file-first fallback ? file-first export pipeline verified end-to-end (`vault_export` ? agent writes file ? grep-able). Materialized `research/videos/2026-03-21_mirofish-?_5SSGximONlY.md` and seeded `research/videos/_index.yaml` for offline browsing. Original "128 videos" assumption was stale (DB now contains only 1 video note); the 135-video content gap is captured as **T116** for a separate background re-ingest.

### Changed
- **T209**: `g-go-code-swarm` and `g-go-swarm` now auto-downgrade to standard single-agent implementation when exactly one runnable item remains after Workspace-Control preflight, while preserving hard blockers for unknown workspace members, non-git-root targets, and unauthorized member writes.
- **T085**: Standardized CRUD verbs across all file/folder record commands ? `g-task-new` ? `g-task-add`, `g-task-update` ? `g-task-upd`, `g-bug-report` ? `g-bug-add`, `g-feat-new` ? `g-feat-add`; old names preserved as deprecated aliases for one version cycle; new `-del` archive commands added for tasks, bugs, features, and constraints; `g-skl-tasks`, `g-skl-bugs`, `g-skl-features`, `g-skl-constraints` updated to reference new verb names; all 10 IDE targets updated
- **T086**: Subsystem CRUD commands ? `g-subsystem-add`, `g-subsystem-upd`, `g-subsystem-del` added; `g-subsystems` now list/status only; `g-skl-subsystems` updated with DEPRECATE operation; all 10 IDE targets
